 The famous Italian artist Maurizio Cattelan named it "comedian"
 isaki keemat 12 xxrep 4 0 dollar yani 85 lakh lagaai gai he
 On Wednesday, it was put on display at Paris' art gallery Parotin, according to a CNN report

 gailaree dwaara instagram par share kiye gaye ek post main kaha gaya he "ye kalakriti is ore ishaara karti he ki ham kisi cheez kaa mulya kis tarah se lagaate hai or kin chizon ko moolyawaan samajhate hai
 "this post also states that the artist Catalan wanted to create a banana-shaped sculpture and always carried a banana in his hotel room to draw inspiration
 xxrep 4 ? Maurizio Cattelan's new sculpture 'comedian' at Art Basel Miami marks the artist's first major debut at an art fair in over 15 years! Comprised of a real banana affixed to the wall with a piece of duct tape, this new work is no different than Cattelan's hyper-realistic sculptures lampooning popular culture and offer a wry commentary on society, power, and authority
 In the same vein as Cattelan's America (2016), this piece offers insight into how we assign worth and what kind of objects we value
 The idea of this work came to the artist's mind a year ago
 Back then, Cattelan was thinking of a sculpture that was shaped like a banana
 Every time he traveled, he brought a banana with him and hung it in his hotel room to find inspiration
 He made several models: first in resin, then in bronze and in painted bronze for finally coming back to the initial idea of a real banana
 Discover it on our booth D24! — Art Basel Miami Beach xxrep 4 ? Perrotin Booth D24 xxrep 4 ? December 5 – 9, 2019 — # mauriziocattelan # artbaselmiami # artbaselmiamibeach # artbasel # Perrotin — Courtesy Maurizio Cattelan
 a post shared by Perrotin Gallery (@galerieperrotin) on Dec 4, 2019 at 5:44 am PST Cattelan has done a lot of banana-related work before using a banana for real
 ye pehla mauka he jab catalan ne beete 15 saalon main kisi art fere ke liye is tarah kii kalakriti banaai he

 3 tivrata kaa bukamp, malbe main dabakar ek mahila kii maut12:43 AM dakshin kashmir ke pulavama main aatanki hamalaa, surakshabalon ke 2 jawan ghayal12:21 AM uttar bengal ke chaar jilon main aaj trade union kii rahegi hadtaal Once, an Arab friend of mine told me that if oil runs out of the Arab land, then nothing can be better for it
 thik usee tarj par kah sakate hai ki bharat main aaj rache ja rahe angreji sahitya ke liye isse acha kuch nahin ho saktaa ki use sadashayi british sangrakshan milanaa band ho jaae
 It was only after the writing of Salman Rushdie and Vikram Seth that British publishers started taking seriously the English writing being done in India
 is baat ko mahaj teen dashak hue hai, lihaaja aisi koi bhi baat kahana jaldbaaji hogi
 Other 'international' publishers (also American) after British publishers also took Indian English writers seriously
 natijatan, pehali baar aisa hua ki 'bhartiya' lekhan aar
 K
 narayan, raja raav yaa anita desai se purvaparichit mutthi bhar samajhadaar pathakon (british, america, bhartiya or anya) ke daayre se baahar niklaa or usne glouci patrikaon ke socity pannon or kitaab kii dukaanon kii rack par apni jagah banaai
 Major international and British publishing agents then had to change their scales to look at Indian English writing
 is prakriya main kuch abhijaat or yuva bhartiya lekhakon ne british or america agenton kaa chakkar lagaana shuru kiya or badi saavdhaanee se unke sampadakon ke saath sahanubhutipurna sampark kaayam kiya
 In return, British agents and literature editors started coming to India, which has turned into an annual literary festival to be held in Jaipur today
 pichley kuch dashakon main jis tareeke se alag-alag rashtriyataon main bandhe is abhijaat saamaajik tabake par bahes kaa khaatmaa hua he, usne inaki ekta ko majboot karne main madad kii he
 This unity looked true, partly because Britain and India share an old relationship
 is maamle main british americanyon se alag hai kyonki america ke bharat se puraane sambandh nahin rahe hai
 Actually, Americans belong to America
 unhen bharat ke angreji lekhan se utani hi ummid ho sakati he jitani kisi or desh main likhe ja rahe angreji sahitya se
 In Britain, the picture is a little different
 vahaan log bharat main likhe ja rahe angreji sahitya se ummid karte hai
 He feels that he knows India
 yah sahi bhi he, lekin isaki aitihaasik simaaen hai
 Indian English writing enjoys British patronage, but due to this incomplete knowledge, the best English literature being composed in India becomes arduous
 yah dudhari talwaar he jo donon taraf se hamaare sarvshereshth ko kaat-chhaant detii he
 The problem is not just that good Indian writers are ignored because they do not fit into the British literature and nationality perspective, but it is that in the eyes of Britain, the best Indian writers are often rejected in India for the wrong reasons
 Huh
